	#Triggered by SOV_nato_war_deadline mission complete_effect
	set_global_flag = SOV_nato_war_over_global
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = EU_member_dynamic
			}
		}
		EU_leave_effect = yes
	}
	SOV = {
		white_peace = GER
		white_peace = ENG
		white_peace = FRA
		set_global_flag = SOV_first_nato_war_victory
		country_event = {
			id = russia.118
			days = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = all_russian_total_mobilization

			remove_ideas = {
				SOV_fratricidal_war

			UKR = {

			remove_idea = SOV_refoming_the_system_4
			add_idea = SOV_refoming_the_system_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_refoming_the_system_5
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SOV_refoming_the_system_5
			add_idea = SOV_refoming_the_system_6
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_refoming_the_system_6
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SOV_refoming_the_system_6
			add_idea = SOV_brand_new_democracy_1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_brand_new_democracy_1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SOV_brand_new_democracy_1
			add_idea = SOV_brand_new_democracy_2
		}
	}
}

SOV_decrease_centralizing_the_system = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = SOV_centralizing_the_system_1
					has_idea = SOV_centralizing_the_system_2
					has_idea = SOV_centralizing_the_system_3
					has_idea = SOV_centralizing_the_system_4
					has_idea = SOV_centralizing_the_system_5

					has_idea = SOV_all_russian_peoples_front_2

	}

SOV_join_ADS = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SOV_ADS_member_flag
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = SOV_ADS_member_flag
		add_ideas = {
			SOV_ADS_member
		}
		remove_ideas = {
			ASEAN_member
			arab_league_member
		}
		SOV = {
			add_to_variable = {
				SOV_ADS_number_of_members = 1
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				SOV_ADS_war_stability_factor_dynamic_var = 0.01
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				SOV_ADS_send_volunteers_tension_dynamic_var = -0.01
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				SOV_ADS_opinion_gain_monthly_same_ideology_factor_dynamic_var = 0.01
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				SOV_ADS_lend_lease_tension_dynamic_var = -0.01
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				SOV_ADS_production_factory_start_efficiency_factor_dynamic_var = 0.005
			}
		}
		add_to_array = {
			SOV.SOV_ads_members = THIS
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SOV
			modifier = friendship_of_peoples
		}
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = friendship_of_peoples
			}
		}
	}
}

SOV_join_brics = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SOV_brics_member_flag
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = SOV_brics_member_flag
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = SOV_solidarity_and_respect
			}
			add_ideas = {
				SOV_brics_member_2
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = {
				SOV_brics_member
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = {
			ASEAN_member
			arab_league_member
		}
		SOV = {
			add_to_variable = {
				SOV_brics_number_of_members = 1
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				SOV_brics_political_power_factor_dynamic_var = 0.005
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				SOV_brics_income_growth_factor_dynamic_var = 0.005
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				SOV_brics_trade_cost_for_target_factor_dynamic_var = -0.005
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				SOV_brics_trade_opinion_factor_dynamic_var = 0.005
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				PRC = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			PRC = {
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_brics_number_of_members = 1
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_brics_political_power_factor_dynamic_var = 0.005
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_brics_income_growth_factor_dynamic_var = 0.005
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_brics_trade_cost_for_target_factor_dynamic_var = -0.005
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_brics_trade_opinion_factor_dynamic_var = 0.005
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_array = {
			SOV.SOV_brics_members = THIS
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SOV
			modifier = friendship_of_peoples
		}	
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = PRC
			modifier = friendship_of_peoples
		}
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PREV
				modifier = friendship_of_peoples
			}
		}
		PRC = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PREV
				modifier = friendship_of_peoples
			}
		}
	}
}

SOV_leave_ADS = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = SOV_ADS_member_flag
		}
		clr_country_flag = SOV_ADS_member_flag
		remove_ideas = {
			SOV_ADS_member
		}
		SOV = {
			add_to_variable = {
				SOV_ADS_number_of_members = -1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						has_completed_focus = SOV_reinstate_comecon
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_ADS_war_stability_factor_dynamic_var = -0.005
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_ADS_send_volunteers_tension_dynamic_var = 0.005
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_ADS_opinion_gain_monthly_same_ideology_factor_dynamic_var = -0.005
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_ADS_lend_lease_tension_dynamic_var = 0.005
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_ADS_war_stability_factor_dynamic_var = -0.01
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_ADS_send_volunteers_tension_dynamic_var = 0.01
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_ADS_opinion_gain_monthly_same_ideology_factor_dynamic_var = -0.01
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					SOV_ADS_lend_lease_tension_dynamic_var = 0.01
				}
			}
		}
		remove_from_array = {
			SOV.SOV_ads_members = THIS
		}
	}
}

		add_to_variable = {
			var = SOV_level_of_exhaustion
			value = 1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_war_exhaustion_war_support_factor_dynamic = -0.05
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_war_exhaustion_army_attack_factor_dynamic = -0.05
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_war_exhaustion_army_defence_factor_dynamic = -0.05
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_war_exhaustion_army_org_factor_dynamic = -0.025
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_war_exhaustion_army_morale_factor_dynamic = -0.05
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SOV_war_exhaustion
				add_idea = SOV_war_exhaustion2
			}
		}
	}
}

SOV_increase_factories = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_a_new_republic
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SOV_more_factories
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_a_new_republic
			has_country_flag = SOV_more_factories
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

SOV_labor_of_love_benefits = {
	random_list = {
		50 = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		50 = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		20 = {

				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1

				}

				add_building_construction = {

					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	hidden_effect = {

SOV_decrease_oligarchy = {
	effect_tooltip = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = SOV_adapt_to_chinese_socialism
					}
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = SOV_developed_socialism
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_kleptocratic_state
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_kleptocratic_state_normal
					add_idea = SOV_kleptocratic_state2_normal
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_kleptocratic_state2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_kleptocratic_state2_normal
					add_idea = SOV_kleptocratic_state3_normal
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_kleptocratic_state3
				}

SOV_increase_government_restructuring = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_1
			add_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_2
			add_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_3
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_3
			add_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_4
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_4
			add_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_government_restructuring_5
		}
		remove_ideas = SOV_government_restructuring_5
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
	}
}

SOV_election_var_balancer = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				target = 1
			}
		}
		divide_temp_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var_temp = 5
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var_temp = -1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var = SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var_temp
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var = SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var_temp
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var = SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var_temp
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				target = 2
			}
		}
		divide_temp_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var_temp = 5
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var_temp = -1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var = SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var_temp
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var = SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var_temp
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var = SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var_temp
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				target = 3
			}
		}
		divide_temp_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var_temp = 5
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var_temp = -1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var = SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var_temp
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var = SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var_temp
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var = SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var_temp
		}
	}
	else = {
		divide_temp_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var_temp = 5
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var_temp = -1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var = SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var_temp
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var = SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var_temp
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var = SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var_temp
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		total_popularity = 0
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		total_popularity = SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		total_popularity = SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		total_popularity = SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		total_popularity = SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				total_popularity > 1
			}
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			total_popularity = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						check_variable = {
							SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var < total_popularity
						}
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var = total_popularity
					}
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						check_variable = {
							SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var < total_popularity
						}
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var = total_popularity
					}
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						check_variable = {
							SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var < total_popularity
						}
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var = total_popularity
					}
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						check_variable = {
							SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var < total_popularity
						}
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var = total_popularity
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				total_popularity < 1
			}
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			total_popularity = 1
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			total_popularity = -1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					add_to_variable = {
						SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var = total_popularity
					}
				}
				10 = {
					add_to_variable = {
						SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var = total_popularity
					}
				}
				10 = {
					add_to_variable = {
						SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var = total_popularity
					}
				}
				10 = {
					add_to_variable = {
						SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var = total_popularity
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var_temp = 0
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var_temp = 0
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var_temp = 0
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var_temp = 0
	}
}

SOV_who_won_the_election = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = {
					SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var > SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var
				}
				check_variable = {
					SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var > SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var
				}
				check_variable = {
					SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var > SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var
				}
				check_variable = {
					SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var > 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = SOV_cprf_won
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = {
					SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var > SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var
				}
				check_variable = {
					SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var > SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var
				}
				check_variable = {
					SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var > SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var
				}
				check_variable = {
					SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var > 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = SOV_ldpr_won
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = {
					SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var > SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var
				}
				check_variable = {
					SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var > SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var
				}
				check_variable = {
					SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var > SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var
				}
				check_variable = {
					SOV_election_approval_rating_srzp_var > 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = SOV_srzp_won
	}
	else = {
		set_global_flag = SOV_medvedev_won
	}
}

SOV_increase_corona = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea4
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea4
			add_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea3
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea3
			add_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea2
			add_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea1
			add_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
	else = {
		add_ideas = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea4
	}
}

SOV_USSR_defeat_in_2nd_European_War = {
	set_global_flag = SOV_nato_second_nato_war_victory_global
	news_event = news.540
	if = {
		limit = {
			FAF = {
				any_war_score > 35
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = FAF_northern_caucasus
	}
	FAF = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = FRA_Lafayette_char
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = france.309
				days = 35
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = FRA_Louis_XX_char
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			country_event = {
